\g CM-hand

\t kɛlɛ bebetsyina kpɛ́ Tingbě mɛ
\m kɛlɛ be-be-tsyina kpɛ́ Tingbě mɛ
\g this 3PL-VENITIVE-turn_round put_in Ewe_language inside

\t Beingbeɛ́ kóŋ́ balɛ bezĩ ki nyéɛ́
\m be-ingbe-ɛ́ kóŋ́ balɛ be-zĩ ki nyé-ɛ́
\g CM:PL-Ewe_people-DEF especially 3PL AM-be_spoilt CM name-DEF

\t begizelũ Tingbě piapíí nɔ́,
\m be-gi-ze-lũ Tingbě piapíí nɔ́
\g 3PL-NEG:PRES-REP-hear Ewe_language well TP

\t bulĩ́ɛ́ kú,
\m bu-lĩ́-ɛ́ kú
\g CM-river-DEF be_high(river)

\t gaké blɔ akaálɛ́ begilũ Tingbě
\m gaké blɔ a-ka-álɛ́ be-gi-lũ Tingbě
\g but 1PL CM-then-PL CM:PL-NEG:PRES-hear Ewe_language

\t piapíí
\m piapíí
\g well

\t kɛlɛ betsyina akpɛ́ sɛ Kumɛ Kumɛ Kumɛ,
\m kɛlɛ be-tsyina a-kpɛ́ sɛ kumɛ kumɛ kumɛ
\g then 3PL-turn_round AM-put_in that Okume Okume Okume
